    _travelconcept, word [-], defn [is (entity(main))]
	    _travelattraction, word [-], defn [is (attraction(sxsw))]
	        park(play), word [n], defn [is (_travelattraction)]
	        nightlife(town), word [n], defn [is (_travelattraction)]
					water(wet), word [n], defn [is (liquid(water), _travelconcept, drink(sip))]
			    _fooddrink, word [-], defn [is (substance(matter), _travelconcept)]
		vehicle(car), word [n], defn [is (_castshadow, _travelconcept)]
			animal(main), word [n], defn [is ("life form"(main), _travelconcept)]
	media(film), word [n], defn [is (entity(main), _travelconcept)]
				music(loud), word [n], defn [is (noise(loud), media(film), _travelconcept)]
			event(party), word [n], defn [is (process(time), attraction(sxsw), _travelconcept, _travelattraction)]
	                                    swim(stroke), word [v, n], defn [is (move(jump), _travelactivity)]
	                                    run(dash), word [v, n], defn [is (move(jump), _travelactivity), has (run(dash).agent(doer), run(dash).speed(fast))] 
						play(sport), word [v], defn [is (participate(in), _travelactivity), has (play(sport).agent(doer), game(cardgame))]
			activity(craft), word [n], defn [is (do(act), _travelactivity)], equiv [_travelactivity]
						sport(game), word [n], defn [is (game(cardgame), _travelactivity), has (game(sport))]
				dance(toes), word [v, n], defn [is (activity(craft), _travelactivity, move(jump))]
				bike(verb), word [v], defn [is (activity(craft), _travelactivity, move(jump))]
				walk(stroll), word [v, n], defn [is (activity(craft), move(jump), _travelactivity)]
				swim(pool), word [v, n], defn [is(_travelactivity)]
				_travelactivity, word [-], defn [is (activity(craft))]
			inactivity(craft), word [n], defn [is (do(act), _travelactivity), not (activity(craft))] 
						college(acc), word [n], equiv [university(alma)], defn [is (_travelconcept, institution(biz))]
		attribute(main), word [n], defn [is (possession(owned), _travelrecommend)]
				film(sxsw), word [n], defn [is (sxsw(austin).part(of), _travelconcept), has (movie(film))]
				interactive(sxsw), word [n], defn [is (sxsw(austin).part(of), _travelconcept), has (topic(main)=technology(tech))]
				music(sxsw), word [n], defn [is (sxsw(austin).part(of), _travelconcept), has (music(loud))]
			_entertainscale, word [-], defn [is (attribute(main), _travelconcept)]
			_musicliveness, word [-], defn [is (attribute(main), _travelconcept)]
			formality(gown), word [n], defn [is (attribute(main), _travelconcept)]
			destination(go), word [n], defn [is (attribute(main))], equiv [_traveldestination]
			    austin(here), word [n], defn [is (_traveldestination)]
				_insideoutside, word [-], defn [is (area(loc), _travelconcept)]
				local(austin), word [adj], defn [is (location(main), _travelconcept)]
				venue(place), word [n], defn [is (location(main), business(biz), _travelconcept), has (fullness(space))]
				volume(sound), word [n], defn [is (attribute(main), _travelconcept)]
				pitch(sound), word [n], defn [is (attribute(main), _travelconcept)]
				temperature(main), word [n], defn [is (quantity(main), _travelconcept)]
						popularity(main), word [n], defn [is (prevalence(main), _travelconcept)]
				duration(time), word [n], defn [is (_traveltime)]
				_traveltime, word [-], equiv[time(season)], defn [is (time(season))]
				time(season), word [n], equiv[duration(time)], defn [is (_traveltime)]
					season(era), word [n], defn [is (time(season), _travelconcept)]
				_moisturelevel, word [-], defn [is (moisture(liquid).quantity(main), _travelconcept)]
                cost(amt), word [n], equiv [price(cost)], defn [is (worth(value), _travelconcept)]
				beauty(cute), word [n], equiv [appealing(pretty), attractive(pretty)], defn [is (good(yay), appearance(style), _travelconcept)]
                quality(goodness), word [n], defn [is (_appealscale, _travelrecommend)]
                        suitable(good), word [adj], defn [is (good(yay), _travelconcept)]
                        friendly(suit), word [adj], equiv [suitable(good)], defn [is (_travelconcept)]
				international(nat), word [adj], defn [is (native(from), _travelconcept)]
				fullness(space), word [n], defn [is (content(in), _travelconcept)]
